<h1>Token Engineering Commons üåæstewards <img src="https://github.com/CommonsBuild/tec-branding-assets/blob/main/Logo/Icon/TEC%20Icon%20Color@2x.png?raw=true"  width="25" height="25" /></h1>

> The main objectives of the Community Stewards WG are to provide visibility across all of the separate work streams such that all Stewards walk forward together in lockstep to reach our high level TEC goals. Our weekly meetings are a place to check-in on the temperature of the community, to resolve blockers, to raise questions that affect the Stewards or the members of our community and to solve them with collective intelligence. We are agile in our planning and follow a 2-week Sprint cadence. [Weekly sync agenda](https://docs.google.com/document/d/1VQNgAThqMLaQrF21uoQabWelnyJKLtX-TbqOl8kVb0Q)

_22-Mar-21 01:39 PM_:

Hi everyone, Nate and I had a meeting discussing the Content and Distribution Strategy. Here are the notes from our call. We will discuss it tomorrow on the weekly sync. **Content Distribution Strategy Meeting (Nate/Marko)** ‚Ä¢ Using Zenhub board in a brand new repo with established content distribution lifecycle (pipeline) [https://github.com/TECommons/content-distribution#workspaces/tec-content-production-and-distribution-60549332d7d741001bbea827/board?repos=349409011](https://github.com/TECommons/content-distribution#workspaces/tec-content-production-and-distribution-60549332d7d741001bbea827/board?repos=349409011) ‚Ä¢ Allow both internal and external contributors to easily submit Ideas and Requests for content distribution. Create a link that automatically opens New Issue on the board with a pre-defined template (issue template draft already created) ‚Ä¢ Medium, Telegram, Forum, Discord (set up bots in between) Need to figure out who will build bots, whomanages them and how to propose edits whenever we need to address CD strategy Who runs the bots? We want to propose a change. Where can we do that? / ask VyVy and Kris ‚Ä¢ Medium: feature other projects within the TE community to publish on our platform and engage others to come to TE community ‚Ä¢ Decide on a central place where all our resources and information can be found with instructions on how to do something (Gitbook, special page on our website, can be public and pass protected for internal resources) ‚Ä¢ We will need to have a person to PM the CD process, Nate volunteer to take it for starters but‚Ä¶ ‚Ä¢ We need to think how to scale regular contributors! (edited)

Deployment of Honey Pot and Celeste Contracts

To update the Honey Pot to integrate with Celeste we have opted to redeploy the entire 1Hive Protocol. This involves deploying a new Aragon DAO in 2 steps between which we will deploy Celeste. This is because the Aragon DAO depends upon Celeste, to allow disputable decisions and proposals, and Celeste depends upon the Aragon DAO, to integrate Br...

_22-Apr-21 07:00 AM_:

Heads up everyone! Figma made changes to how they handle Free accounts and limitations for projects/pages etc. With this new change all free accounts are allowed max 3 projects, files and pages. We are now forced to upgrade Team account for at least one member if we want to keep it organised all under one roof. For that reason I moved all Team files **back** to my personal account where I pay the annual subscription and we have no limitations of how many files we can create. That being said, some old links to Figma files that have been shared elsewhere will no longer open.

Hi all! In light of Eth CC in Paris in July, here are the new rules on traveling to France as of June 9:

Permissions to travel to France:

Countries are grouped into three colors.

GREEN -¬†EU, Switzerland, Australia, South Korea, Israel, Japan, Lebanon, New Zealand, Singapore: no PCR requirement if fully vaccinated

ORANGE - Most other countries including UK and US: 72 h PCR or rapid test 48h¬† vaccinated or not. If not vaccinated, travel only for ‚Äúurgent and necessary reasons" ("motifs imp√©rieux‚Äù which means death in the family, etc. with proof) and must self-isolate 7 days


RED - South Africa and India: "motif imp√©rieux" (again, "urgent and necessary reasons") even if vaccinated. PCR under 48 H or rapid test. Mandatory 10 day quarantine if not vaccinated or self isolation 7 days if vaccinated.

_08-Jun-21 05:19 AM_:

I agree with Sem. People need to fully understand the implications of these types of voting decisions. We can get away with low voter turnout if we KNOW that proper communication AND education on the topic was presented to the community effectively. Also capturing the elements of what makes this decision worthy of a community vote is something we should evaluate. If we consider this vote to be legitimate on the grounds of community education and awareness, I would say no, its not legitimate.

Thank you, @liviade, for questioning the unanimous yes vote. It's good that we are asking ourselves this. My yes vote was based on the following assumptions: 1. I have a high level understanding of the mechanics and advantages, enough to believe this is worth trying. 2. In the case a serious blocker surfaces, we can shift to an in-house method. 3. Proposals by @sem(üå∏,üêù) carry additional weight for me, personally, because he is always so thoughtful and analytical 3. Trust in Soft Gov, Gravity and Commons Swarm to execute this in the community's best interest.

For example: one question I cannot answer myself: if as a TE you contributed in TEC, but won't participate in this or in other CS hatches, why do you need to be part of the Association? If the Association is set up to provide legal protection for hatchers, why must TE contributors become members?

<h3>liviade <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/480023322080444427/5749f33d32f3d2bf7084c18540ead477.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_09-Jun-21 03:54 PM_:

The Association was chosen as the TEC legal strategy by the legal working group for a few reasons : 1. Liability is to cover every hatcher, someone not under legal protection could be a possible risk/liability. 2. The Trusted Seed ensures value aligned Hatchers and has a single process for everyone involved. It lowers the overhead and increases legitimacy to not open exceptions. It is a choice to participate in the hatch under this conditions and anyone can participate after the Commons Upgrade. The scholarships are offered so there is no block for any trusted member that wants to be involved. Here is most of our legal documentation [https://app.gitbook.com/@token-engineering-commons/s/tec-handbook/hatch-101/legal](https://app.gitbook.com/@token-engineering-commons/s/tec-handbook/hatch-101/legal)

Tokenlog ¬∑ Token-weighted backlogs

Democratize your open-source software project. A better way for projects to collaborate with their biggest supporters.

![https://tokenlog.xyz/icon.png](https://tokenlog.xyz/icon.png)

any proposals on what to do?

I have a few...

#1 <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f6ab.png" width=50 height=50> <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f47d.png" width=20 height=20>

We call it in the call as we planned no matter how close the results are... Livia reloads live and boom thats the answer.... (edited)

Various other options that i see we have and some can be mixed and matched: #2 We follow the Disputable Voting pattern that we have in the Commons final arrangement... its called "wait for quiet" where if there is a flip in the final result in the last 24 hours, then there is 24 more hours extended for voters that havent voted yet. #3 We extend it 24 hours and thats it #4 We close the 2 issues that people voted on that are clearly out of the running #5 We do a full runoff over the weekend, closing all votes and only putting up Fire and No Aliens #6 We combine the votes for the 2 non-intervention and intervention (a horrible idea please lets not do this but i'm saying it anyway)

Any other mechanisms we should consider?

is counted as people's IH and ~50% impact hours from <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f6ab.png" width=50 height=50> <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f47d.png" width=20 height=20>

_08-Jul-21 08:35 AM_:

[https://forum.tecommons.org/t/pre-hatch-impact-hours-distribution-analysis/376/50?u=liviade](https://forum.tecommons.org/t/pre-hatch-impact-hours-distribution-analysis/376/50?u=liviade) There is a support for solution #7 here: **What if there is a polarized scenario, where 2 different proposals have an evenly split majority of votes in the run-off?** (By evenly split, we consider a difference of less than 10 votes between first and second place.) In this case, the top 2 authors will be invited to a hack session to merge their proposals together and commit to a collaborative result. - My bad for putting 10 votes there. I wish I had added a larger margin because we are still gonna be polarized even with 100 or 200 votes splitting first and second place

I think that if we choose any of the proposals like they are, there will be a lot of conflict around legitimacy and there will be people feeling good but also there will be people feeling bad about the decision. I like #7 as proposes a dialogue to not foster polarization, i think we should try to flip this into a win-win escenario, and not a splitting decision.

_08-Jul-21 10:30 AM_:

Honestly, I believe that this whole process of now trying to change something backwards has added more conflict than benefit. I just do not see any option where at least someone will not feel confortable with. There is no perfect solution because there are many different cases. No matter what you do, some people will feel not being treated fair. I believe we should try to "compensate" looking forward and not backward. For instance adding the governance power and adding some IH to those members we believe they deserve some, but not taking IH from those who have them. Adding is fair, taking away is not, no matter if the system was not perfect, they did not design the system and were playing the rules. (edited)

_08-Jul-21 10:46 AM_:

The Cultural Build is an experiment of a collaborative and self managed organization which is implementing Ostrom's 8 principles into our culture. We are doing something for the first time. We have always taken the posture of looking into how things are moving, and if change is needed, change can be proposed. The results of this analys and votes are surfacing so many behavioral challenges that we still need to learn how to navigate. We can't have a set in stone tradition before even launching. There is a need for flexibility when in experimental grounds

<h3>santigs <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/434632218246381569/ecb10317edc17d2e273d2404cc6f6a52.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_08-Jul-21 10:57 AM_:

Just look at the voting system right now. We are using a voting process and then when we see two options quite close in votes, we decide we need to change the overall result to take into account those not voting the winning proposal. I am not against that, but we are changing the rules again just because we do not feel the outcome is fair. When you vote using a voting process, you respect the rules in that process, if you do not like the final outcome you then decide if you feel represented in the community and decide what you want to do as a member and as a community, you decide if you want to change the process in cases where the top options are almost tied in votes, but you do not change the result of the voting, the voting process should not be changed in that decision, it should be changed afterwards for future voting.

<h3>Zeptimus <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/183879548394274816/5e45f3338bd1b9a2a524cde1083166f6.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_08-Jul-21 12:01 PM_:
Some people have IH taken away in Praisemageddon.. I think it would be a lot easier to discuss this if we could ignore the outcome a bit and as Santi says, look ahead. Right now, no proposal has a majority of votes. not even close... the top voted proposal has ~40%. This has been a horrible horrible experience for our community. I regret that we even debated this. I really do. We have an extremely polarized community right now. This shit is like democrats vs republicans in the states, it's gross.

![https://cdn.discordapp.com/emojis/496084055532634142.gif](https://cdn.discordapp.com/emojis/496084055532634142.gif)

We have to think about what is best for the Commons. #7 allows everyone to win a little bit, which is just the best that we can do right now. Instead of a clearly defined set of winners and losers, we can have both sides opinions represented in the final outcome. Honestly, this whole time I have been watching this as a train wreck waiting to happen, i never saw a way to push the car off the track... Amazingly, I think we can actually "Split the baby in half" and it will work out. (google it if you don't know what i'm talking about) I have had a lot of anxiety about this, and when Livia brainstormed with me and this idea popped out, it was the first time in weeks that i felt hope around this topic. That we could actually have a solution that doesnt completely just disregard a large swath of our community. I'm not happy about an intervention at all, I never thought it was a good idea, we should have clearly laid out the rules in advance if we wanted to do that and then stuck with them IMO it's too late to change the rules and decide to take from some to give to others. But that is not everyone's opinion and I really love that we have a community of diverse opinions. Looking forward, COMPROMISE is a value that will hold us together better than accepting the vile, false dichotomies of democrat vs republican, socialist vs libertarian, Good vs bad, right vs wrong. There is no "good" here, there is no "right" here. There is only best... Compromise is something I think we as a community can be proud of, and it is at the very least in the spirit of the rules as set forth for this process, if not explicitly defined as the solution for a polarized outcome.


Sorry for the rant... I will also post in the forum

_08-Jul-21 01:10 PM_:

I was referring to Tam's analysis - forgive me 8 in the context of "before the extension" "8 out of 30 voters (27%) cast 50% of the total votes." [https://forum.tecommons.org/t/pre-hatch-impact-hours-distribution-analysis/376/81](https://forum.tecommons.org/t/pre-hatch-impact-hours-distribution-analysis/376/81) "it would require 10 of 37 voters, 27% of voters, alone to determine the winner. If all other 27 voters combined, 73% of voters, voted for a single but different option, they would not have enough votes to pass it. Before the 24h extension: 8 out of 30 voters (27%) cast 50% of the total votes. After the 24h extension: 10 out of 37 voters (27%) cast 50% of the total votes." And Jeff's original analysis, which I know you were trying to categorize differently. The point is, there is a small # who have a large impact of governance in the builder's pool. 5/8/10 people in the kind of voter turnout we have to sway the vote that much, isn't a % I would like to see in a community I am co-vested in. That is my opinion. (edited)

_14-Jul-21 11:07 AM_:

Hi @solsista there is a "WG readiness for Hatch" checklist and zenhub list that we've been tracking in the Stewards call for the past few weeks and sharing in the weekly Community sync. It is to highlight all the remaining issues that would **block** us from Hatching! Since 0mega does not have any Hatch blocking issues, I defaulted it to ready. When we started tracking there were a number of working groups that were not yet ready: Community Stewards, Soft Gov, Hatch Outreach, Comms, TEC Params, Commons Swarm, Legal and Labs. And so these were really where all the focus went. Week by week the ready signals were given and now, as @liviade mentioned above, the last remaining task is the final IH list! Thanks for jumping in to ask and I apologize if you thought there was another step you needed to do!!

_20-Aug-21 10:22 AM_:

This Bankless ep was dedicated to DAOs. The guests shared some insights I found sparked different thought paths for me. The conversation flows from leadership to sucess metrics to DAO lifestyles to onboarding as a common pain point for all DAOs. Not everything pesonally resonated but I would still recommend giving it a listen. Howdy, @Stewards and gang! This message comes from the collective of @anna-marie @Edu - TEC Steward. and myself along with @nic @Vyvy-vi and @natesuits to share here with you the hopeful creation of a new working group to support orientation and community building: I present to you the Communitas WG Manifesto! <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f31f.png" width=20 height=20>

We hope to talk about it tomorrow at Stewards and share with you now for advice process and such. Thank you! <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f64f.png" width=20 height=20>

[https://docs.google.com/document/d/1g9vycoqIZkg83KyRM-7wMeCN-QxZTSfO-Ofq8o7U9pQ

Communitas WG Manifesto v.0.1

Communitas Working Group Manifesto ‚ÄãCommunitas (n., Latin) - commonly referring either to an unstructured community in which people are equal, or to the very spirit of community. ‚ÄúCommunitas refers to an unstructured state in which all members of a community are equal, allowing them to share a ...

Hi @Stewards As mentioned on our weekly yday, the Stewards Council will start on Sept 23. <h3>innov8tor3 <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/530682470232883210/193353ccfcbc44b9892dbb7a5862c455.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_22-Sep-21 01:45 AM_:

Hey @Tam2140 , you were asking for project managers on your wish list. I've done some work with @anna-marie , so that's one point of reference. I'm also just on Graviton Training, Cohort 2, and loving what you guys are doing, with specific issues I want and need to resolve. In the corporate world, I was project manager of an end to end product and service delivery supply chain where we added 100,000 customers at a major UK Telco over two years. I tended not to use Kanban, because I feel that project participants need "their own channels" structured using their own language. But then relating each channel, so channels don't become silos. I see that here! That approach, plus a consultative / collaborative mindset, meant a much higher than average success rate. That could have been luck, or some kind of instinct, but it felt right. My challenge has been and still is to adapt that to open, diverse networks eg in Twitter and Discord. Luckily, I love learning. Also luckily, there's so much to learn here. I can already see Gravity WG applications in other DAOs. I'm like a kid in a sweety shop! How shall we engage from here?



<h3>innov8tor3 <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/530682470232883210/193353ccfcbc44b9892dbb7a5862c455.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

I'm also just on Graviton Training, Cohort 2, and loving what you guys are doing, with specific issues I want and need to resolve. In the corporate world, I was project manager of an end to end product and service delivery supply chain where we added 100,000 customers at a major UK Telco over two years. I tended not to use Kanban, because I feel that project participants need "their own channels" structured using their own language. But then relating each channel, so channels don't become silos. The first official vote of the Hatch DAO has started. **The vote ends on 00:25 UTC on 3 Oct. (i.e., Oct. 3 @ 2:25 AM CET)** The purpose is to ratify the signalling vote that was taken on Snapshot. The signalling vote was to determine whether or not to even submit it to the Hatch DAO. It passed with 100% voting ‚Äúyes‚Äù. _01-Oct-21 12:54 PM_:

**Human Verification Proposal**

With discord's new features and how they have been developing(ephemeral messages and interactions, slash commands), a new verification workflow is possible, which makes it safer to do it right inside discord and make it more intuitive, so that anyone could join without much issues :)

## What is this? New users enter the sever, and they need to agree to the rules at the screen that pops up before they could do things in the server. After that they will have to click on a button in `#verification`, and select an answer from the dropdown. If they answer correctly, the bot assignes a "human" or "verified" role to them ## The cons of using this - - This might not work for people with outdated discord clients, since this was added like 3-4 months ago. (*though, discord auto-updates, and is usually up-to-date for most people*) - If anyone gets stuck, they'll have to DM someone to get access. (We would need some people who would be interested in assigning people the 'human'/'verified' role, if they're stuck) - Random errors could crash the bot (this isn't pitch perfect as of yet, since my friend(https://github.com/nhcarrigan) like made this new bot in 30-40 mins). ## The Pros of this - - Waaaay better than the captcha site. The user experience in this method is super smooth, and ensures that joining isn't a hassle. - One solution, instead of a split-solution. (the captcha site was a site, plus a bot) - This is cooool! - Unifies the rules-agreement and the verification into one source, rather than needing to react to a message by CarlBot. - UserSafety and Privacy ++ This won't need people to use discord auth to sign up(which can be slightly scary for a few people). Nothing get's stored by this, and all data is contained between discord, due to which we won't need to make legal Terms of Service and Usage documents

Here's a video showing the walkthrough -

[https://file.coffee/u/V1GBsAQaPMvykR.mov](https://file.coffee/u/V1GBsAQaPMvykR.mov)





<h3>Tam2140 <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/751417874886688798/2654f95ffa0a47282c16ea274733b86d.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

<h3>Vyvy-vi <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/558192816308617227/af64b80c32205d256106f8da7e88a3ce.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

**Human Verification Proposal** With discord's new features and how they have been developing(ephemeral messages and interactions, slash commands), a new verification workflow is possible, which makes it safer to do it right inside discord and make it more intuitive, so that anyone could join without much issues :)

## What is this? New users enter the sever, and they need to agree to the rules at the screen that pops up before they could do things in the server. After that they will have to click on a button in `#verification`, and select an answer from the dropdown. If they answer correctly, the bot assignes a "human" or "verified" role to them ## The cons of using this - - This might not work for people with outdated discord clients, since this was added like 3-4 months ago. (*though, discord auto-updates, and is usually up-to-date for most people*) - If anyone gets stuck, they'll have to DM someone to get access. (We would need some people who would be interested in assigning people the 'human'/'verified' role, if they're stuck) - Random errors could crash the bot (this isn't pitch perfect as of yet, since my friend(https://github.com/nhcarrigan) like made this new bot in 30-40 mins). ## The Pros of this - - Waaaay better than the captcha site. The user experience in this method is super smooth, and ensures that joining isn't a hassle. - One solution, instead of a split-solution. (the captcha site was a site, plus a bot) - This is cooool! - Unifies the rules-agreement and the verification into one source, rather than needing to react to a message by CarlBot. - UserSafety and Privacy ++ This won't need people to use discord auth to sign up(which can be slightly scary for a few people). Nothing get's stored by this, and all data is contained between discord, due to which we won't need to make legal Terms of Service and Usage documents

Here's a video showing the walkthrough -

[https://file.coffee/u/V1GBsAQaPMvykR.mov](https://file.coffee/u/V1GBsAQaPMvykR.mov)

<h3>Tam2140 <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/751417874886688798/2654f95ffa0a47282c16ea274733b86d.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

<h3>Vyvy-vi <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/558192816308617227/af64b80c32205d256106f8da7e88a3ce.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

**Human Verification Proposal** With discord's new features and how they have been developing(ephemeral messages and interactions, slash commands), a new verification workflow is possible, which makes it safer to do it right inside discord and make it more intuitive, so that anyone could join without much issues :)

## What is this? New users enter the sever, and they need to agree to the rules at the screen that pops up before they could do things in the server. After that they will have to click on a button in `#verification`, and select an answer from the dropdown. If they answer correctly, the bot assignes a "human" or "verified" role to them ## The cons of using this - - This might not work for people with outdated discord clients, since this was added like 3-4 months ago. (*though, discord auto-updates, and is usually up-to-date for most people*) - If anyone gets stuck, they'll have to DM someone to get access. (We would need some people who would be interested in assigning people the 'human'/'verified' role, if they're stuck) - Random errors could crash the bot (this isn't pitch perfect as of yet, since my friend(https://github.com/nhcarrigan) like made this new bot in 30-40 mins). ## The Pros of this - - Waaaay better than the captcha site. The user experience in this method is super smooth, and ensures that joining isn't a hassle. - One solution, instead of a split-solution. (the captcha site was a site, plus a bot) - This is cooool! - Unifies the rules-agreement and the verification into one source, rather than needing to react to a message by CarlBot. - UserSafety and Privacy ++ This won't need people to use discord auth to sign up(which can be slightly scary for a few people). Nothing get's stored by this, and all data is contained between discord, due to which we won't need to make legal Terms of Service and Usage documents

Here's a video showing the walkthrough -

[https://file.coffee/u/V1GBsAQaPMvykR.mov](https://file.coffee/u/V1GBsAQaPMvykR.mov)

<h3>ALOYSIOUS <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/778446953004007475/66df964f1e36116bca7844247c896564.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

Rewards System Process The purpose of this system is to create a way to record, reward and analyze fairly the work done by contributors to the TEC, creating a manner of providing decentralized updates of the action happening in the Commons. _16-Oct-21 03:31 AM_:

gm @ALOYSIOUS ! New working groups form rather organically. There is no formal proposal needed and we have a checklist (thanks to @Vyvy-vi and @freshelle) that anyone can use to launch a new WG. It can use some refinement but it does contain the pieces of work to be done for a smoother integration of the new WG. [https://docs.google.com/document/d/19CgtAf9pVzUApcduzprwE_1M2lsaNG6wvSBUHEmEKJs

Checklist for Creating a New Working Groups (TEC)

About This checklist includes the actions needed in creating a new Working Group (WG) for TEC. This serves as a guide on how to properly set-up a new WG. The steward of the WG must ensure the fulfillment of most, if not all, of the checklist. Primary Write the Working Group‚Äôs manifesto. Exam...

[https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/yUaFtqkjq2bFNcsqsHB6pZNbqreJ1M078dpRJEGt0tLImK_IaNP5eyhyCybIL08Y7HU2ve9aGm9_2A=w1200-h630-p](https://lh3.googleusercontent.com/yUaFtqkjq2bFNcsqsHB6pZNbqreJ1M078dpRJEGt0tLImK_IaNP5eyhyCybIL08Y7HU2ve9aGm9_2A=w1200-h630-p)

Community Stewards Working Group Manifesto

The Initial Buy-In

Proposal Title The Initial Buy-in Proposal Information We want to be the first buyers on our Augmented Bonding Curve (ABC)! This proposal aims to acquire TEC tokens at the moment of initialization of the ABC in order to allow the TEC to acquire tokens at the lowest possible price for key allocations. We will outline what these tokens may be u...

hey @Stewards as Zep pointed out this week, we need to look into Snapshot params for approving a proposal - I just made this forum post with a few polls inside so we can get this started [https://forum.tecommons.org/t/snapshot-params/674](https://forum.tecommons.org/t/snapshot-params/674)

Snapshot Params

What should be the parameters for a proposal to pass on Snapshot? Snapshot is a token weighted voting tool going to be used for: Large impact cultural decisions Community signal Runoff votes (coming from crowd proposal making on Tokenlog) As of now, only TECH holders can submit proposals. We can‚Äôt program params into Snapshot (not that I know...

_29-Oct-21 08:35 PM_:
Hey gang. Just wanted to send a personal note that I will be stepping back from the stewards role in preparation for WG budgets after upgrade. Hopefully only a temporary move, but you never know. Life is full, and happily so. Work, family, play...not enough hours in a day, ultimately. Truly an honor to have collaborated with this amazing group of people and supported our growing community over the past 14 months. Little did I know the glory I would find when I hesitantly joined the very first community call. A steward? Heck yes! And the story evolves. Not going anywhere and will continue to engage as life allows, just relinquishing the stewards moniker <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f913.png" width=20 height=20>

![https://cdn.discordapp.com/emojis/850673915441315880.png](https://cdn.discordapp.com/emojis/850673915441315880.png)

_01-Nov-21 09:16 AM_:

I think a better solution, instead of voting on people directly, would be to vote on groups of people

so it doesn't make anyone directly vulnerable and uncomfortable

and we have a holistic view of the final configuration

The way I see this working is: 1. create a bullet point list with all the responsibilities multi-sig holders will have 2. Send to everyone you would like to include and ask them to give a thumbs up if they agree to take on those responsibilities 3. randomize the people who said yes into 5 different groups 4. submit to snapshot a ranked choice voting for this groups 5. the integrants of top group will be in the multisig

_01-Nov-21 11:20 AM_:

Okay just to keep everyone informed we had an impromptu meeting with Zeptimus, Myself, Ivi, Livi and Edu to discuss how to move forward with the buy-in. We reached consensus around a **ranked choice voting** round to decide who will sit on the multisig - community members can nominate or self-nominate, nominee have 2 days to respond (if it takes longer than 2 days they probably aren't a good candidate. By this means the community will decide the members and composition (hatchers vs. stewards) the blocker for this process will be Livi posting a proposal and subsequent voting for what types of voting methods we can use followed by the vote for the buy-in proposal which will be a simple yes/no(/abstain?) quadratic vote given the buy-in proposal passes we make a third proposal for the multisig composition


<h3>mitch (üçî, üçî) <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/288019500132073472/f2a7e7eb583ccb9397f85406a3962ec3.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

Okay just to keep everyone informed we had an impromptu meeting with Zeptimus, Myself, Ivi, Livi and Edu to discuss how to move forward with the buy-in. We reached consensus around a **ranked choice voting** round to decide who will sit on the multisig - community members can nominate or self-nominate, nominee have 2 days to respond (if it takes longer than 2 days they probably aren't a good candidate. By this means the community will decide the members and composition (hatchers vs. stewards) the blocker for this process will be Livi posting a proposal and subsequent voting for what types of voting methods we can use followed by the vote for the buy-in proposal which will be a simple yes/no(/abstain?) quadratic vote given the buy-in proposal passes we make a third proposal for the multisig composition

Okay just to keep everyone informed we had an impromptu meeting with Zeptimus, Myself, Ivi, Livi and Edu to discuss how to move forward with the buy-in. We reached consensus around a **ranked choice voting** round to decide who will sit on the multisig - community members can nominate or self-nominate, nominee have 2 days to respond (if it takes longer than 2 days they probably aren't a good candidate. By this means the community will decide the members and composition (hatchers vs. stewards) the blocker for this process will be Livi posting a proposal and subsequent voting for what types of voting methods we can use followed by the vote for the buy-in proposal which will be a simple yes/no(/abstain?) quadratic vote given the buy-in proposal passes we make a third proposal for the multisig composition

<h3>liviade <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/480023322080444427/5749f33d32f3d2bf7084c18540ead477.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_01-Nov-21 06:44 PM_:

What would this look like if was simple? We already have one nomination for the complete multisig. It's just one nomination. Let's get more. The rationale behind the nomination was explained. Cool. That's helpful for the community to understand and vote on. Why not have an open call to the community to submit ‚Äúnomination sets‚Äù and explain their reasons why? Then 2-3 or even 5-6 people or even more people spend the time to consider what rationale is important to them for this responsibility. Then they find the 7 persons that match that criteria, reach out to ask and explain and, if all agree, they submit that nomination set. Then we have a group of nomination sets. And we vote on them. A monimation set if a group of 7 persons that each: - Hold one or more TECH tokens - Understand and agree to the responsibilities of the role The responsibilities of the role are (This is an off the cuff draft and can be improved): - Respond within 24 hours of a request to use the multisig. - Verify the allocation request was passed by the community (specifying exactly how would be useful here. For the present, let‚Äôs say it‚Äôs comparing the snapshot vote and the parameters required to pass.) - Alert the other multisig holders when you will be unavailable for a 24h or greater period of time - Uphold the values of the TEC - Spread joy (this is not actually a really real responsibility but it sure would be nice).

_02-Nov-21 12:54 PM_:
You know, @Zeptimus , you and and I might have different points of view on a coupla things but where we always align is that it‚Äôs in the hands of the community to decide. <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f642.png" width=50 height=50> <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f64c.png" width=50 height=50> <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f3fd.png" width=20 height=20>

In this case, it looks like the community should probably have a say in how a group is selected for community multisigs (differentiated from the multisigs of WGs). Especially as this may not only set a precedent but may be

**The**

protocol moving forward. There are at least 3 options so far: (1) individuals nominate or self-nominate and then they are listed in a rank choice vote, (2) individuals nominate a group from all token holders (and do the leg work of assuring there is consent and share their rationale for the nomination so the voting community can make an informed decision) and (3) individuals nominate a group from the Steward group.

<h3>Tam2140 <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/751417874886688798/2654f95ffa0a47282c16ea274733b86d.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

In this case, it looks like the community should probably have a say in how a group is selected for community multisigs (differentiated from the multisigs of WGs). Especially as this may not only set a precedent but may be **The** protocol moving forward. There are at least 3 options so far: (1) individuals nominate or self-nominate and then they are listed in a rank choice vote, (2) individuals nominate a group from all token holders (and do the leg work of assuring there is consent and share their rationale for the nomination so the voting community can make an informed decision) and (3) individuals nominate a group from the Steward group. <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f642.png" width=50 height=50> <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f64c.png" width=50 height=50> <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f3fd.png" width=20 height=20>

<h3>Zeptimus <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/183879548394274816/5e45f3338bd1b9a2a524cde1083166f6.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_02-Nov-21 01:01 PM_:
yeah! ofc im just giving my opinion thats what i always say community must decide <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f609.png" width=20 height=20>

its good to have different opinions it enriches our culture and make it stronger


<h3>Tam2140 <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/751417874886688798/2654f95ffa0a47282c16ea274733b86d.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

You know, @Zeptimus , you and and I might have different points of view on a coupla things but where we always align is that it‚Äôs in the hands of the community to decide.   In this case, it looks like the community should probably have a say in how a group is selected for community multisigs (differentiated from the multisigs of WGs). Especially as this may not only set a precedent but may be **The** protocol moving forward. There are at least 3 options so far: (1) individuals nominate or self-nominate and then they are listed in a rank choice vote, (2) individuals nominate a group from all token holders (and do the leg work of assuring there is consent and share their rationale for the nomination so the voting community can make an informed decision) and (3) individuals nominate a group from the Steward group. <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f642.png" width=50 height=50> <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f64c.png" width=50 height=50> <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f3fd.png" width=20 height=20>

_03-Nov-21 03:25 AM_:

it seems "important things" to "organizational" aspects of TE Commons, need more active Stewards than the initial 3-4 hrs per week, check-in once a week, take care of a topic/WG etc. Just a thought I'm carrying around for some time now. On the other hand "operational upgrades", like using multisigs, funding etc. maybe require more participatory communication opportunities and should not be dealt in the same flow/stream of work as "regular" day-to-day getting things done mode? Also, please do not take my comment any wrong way, I'm trying to map the different speeds - and how informed participation can take place (from a more generic PoV, caring about multiple communities etc.). Imagine if people investing 3-4 hours per week, contribute insights, engage with the community etc. have difficulties with "informed participation" how is it going to be for any TE community member?

maybe a "better dashboard" ? A "catchphrase" in the post title, etc.

_03-Nov-21 04:29 AM_:

Thanks for these insights, @solsista. The original time commitments does indeed feel low and agree there is a difference between those Stewards that are more involved in day-to-day versus those leading more autonomous WGs like 0mega. These ideas are being fleshed out in the Stewards WG funding proposal. For example, WG Coordination Leads (WGCL) have min of 10 hours/wk expected as they are expected to particiapte in our coordination events. Most actually spend multiples of that. I welcome any thought or comments you want to drop in here as we think about how to fund the efforts of Stewards and the coordination efforts made. There are still some pieces to be better thought through. [https://docs.google.com/document/d/1Df96GptjepEDRJCK4bI6BCnr0KfQNaPpVsMLCCb6qwY

_05-Nov-21 06:39 AM_:

The main objective of the Community Stewards WG is to provide visibility across all of the separate work streams such that all Stewards walk forward together in lockstep to reach our high level TEC goals. Our weekly meetings are a place to check-in on the temperature of the community, to resolve blockers, to raise questions that affect the Stewards or the members of our community and to solve them with the collective intelligence. We follow a Scrum framework and have a 2-week Sprint cadence. WG Lead: @Tam2140 Discussions happen on #stewards channel All calls happen on #stewards voice channel Weekly call: Tuesday at 7pm CET Council call: Every other Thursday at 6pm CET Sprint Retrospective: Every other Thursday at 6pm CET Sprint Planning: Every other Friday at 6pm CET Stewards Manifesto [https://docs.google.com/document/d/1cqdURiW7Qv50J_Ha9FLr9IvdqnZGuhlsffL6O1ivHnA

Community Stewards Working Group Manifesto

Community Stewards WG Manifesto Table of Contents Members 2 Stewards and Working Group Coordination Leads (WGCL) 3 Funding 3 Terms 3 Commitments 4 Goals 5 What goals would you like to achieve with this working group? 5 How will this working group benefit the TEC community according to its ...

[https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/hBKMc_onrcHFab745J9zKUKSD9tnfkPRnz1DRhwKOV96_BO0OaZW7Ev94ozgMs5SqwNQUqdHFcOLAg=w1200-h630-p](https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/hBKMc_onrcHFab745J9zKUKSD9tnfkPRnz1DRhwKOV96_BO0OaZW7Ev94ozgMs5SqwNQUqdHFcOLAg=w1200-h630-p)

I am voicing here and cross-posted in the Comms channel - I feel it is not appropriate to use Twitter from the voice of a "decentralized DAO/Commons" to promote proposal/objectives (be political). Will Tweets go out to urge to pass *every proposal? Notification of proposals is important to keep people up to date, but showing favoritism or saying "this is our objective" is basically saying that every person in the TEC has this perspective, which again, I think is not the right use of this platform. Thank you for your consideration and would love to hear feedback. (edited)

_04-Feb-22 06:11 AM_:

A clear example of "co-opting" as political scientists would put it. When factions within wider rivalrous structures appraise common resources (in this case comms channels) to lobby in their favour. I'd say this is reminiscent of the "rewards discussion" or previous dismemberment of agreements made on rewards distribution before the hatch. Just saying because the TEC as an organic structure will continue to mimic its own flaws.

[https://token-engineering-commons.gitbook.io/tec-source/](https://token-engineering-commons.gitbook.io/tec-source/)

Welcome to TEC Source

TEC Source is here to provide easy access to active and archived documents within the TEC. If you are currently working on a document and want to share it here, please notify one of our Stewards!

_24-Feb-22 09:18 AM_:

Hey, I was thinking about yesterday's conversation and I think it's a good opportunity to let something out that I've been thinking about as well.


After some recent changes and discussions at 1Hive, they want to focus on Gardens and organizational apps, so Honeyswap is somewhat out of the equation.

Maybe TEC (or perhaps a new DAO) wants to take Honeyswap and build some features for the Commons like integrating ABCs into the aggregator and many other things that may come out after some brainstorming.

One advantage I guess is that Honeyswap is still the second largest DEX on a chain that's building momentum, i'll just leave that there and hopefully it sparks some conversation.

In our Communitas call today, we agreed that it made sense to share this document with Stewards and even ping a few of you who might be particularly interested ( @liviade, @Zeptimus, @griff (üíú, üíú), @chuygarcia.eth, @natesuits, @Juankbell, @akrtws (TE Academy) ). This doc started as a plan for Communitas but the first half of it evolved into a bigger exploration of how the TEC relates to it people over time. This bigger frame is intentionally ambitious - not a concrete plan so much as a framework that can serve as catalyst for conversation, and then--if it makes sense-- turned into actual plans. I recommend commenting directly in the document as a first step in the conversation. Here it is: [https://docs.google.com/document/d/1U56cG2uAN2zPpDVEdDwVqlxjSFQMJ2KhDyrbCvdWvcc

The TEC and Its People

The TEC and Its People This is a framework for thinking about how the TEC relates to its community members. It is intended as an evolution of not just the Communitas working group, but the TEC as a whole. The brushstrokes of this plan are broad and intentionally bold. It is meant to inspire us to...

Following the stewards call today I decided to add in our discussion topics to the existing thread for the TEC as a payer for the proposal inverter proposal - [https://forum.tecommons.org/t/dogfooding-the-proposal-inverter-tec-as-a-payer-funder-sponsor/804/7](https://forum.tecommons.org/t/dogfooding-the-proposal-inverter-tec-as-a-payer-funder-sponsor/804/7) I think it's the best way to quickly get the most context on the issue and keep it all in one place.

Dogfooding the Proposal Inverter - TEC as a payer(funder/sponsor)

_23-Mar-22 03:15 PM_:

want to share this fragment of a chapter about copyright CC and peer production licences: "A copyfarleft license must allow commons-based commercial use while denying the ability to profit by exploiting wage labour. The copyleft Non-Commercial approach does neither, it prevents commons-based commerce, while restricting wage exploitation only by requiring the exploiters to share some loot with the so-called original author. In no way does this overcome the iron law for either the authors or other workers. ‚ÄòNon Commercial‚Äô is not a suitable way to describe the required endogenic/exogenic boundary. Yet, no other commons license exists that provides a suitable legal framework for commons-based producers to use. Only a license that effectively prevents alienated property and wage labour from being employed in the reproduction of the otherwise free information commons can change the distribution of wealth. Interestingly, this is the correct application of the original institution of the commons, which was strictly related to material production (even reiterating this characteristic in today‚Äôs cultural debate sounds grotesque to many). The commons were land used by a specific community to harvest or breed their animals. If someone could not send cows to pasture and produce milk on it, it would not be considered a real commons. Kleiner argues that if money cannot be made from it, a culturalwork does not belong to the commons: it is still private property." Matteo Pasquinelli [https://www.academia.edu/1992023/Animal_Spirits_A_Bestiary_of_the_Commons](https://www.academia.edu/1992023/Animal_Spirits_A_Bestiary_of_the_Commons)

<h3>iviangita <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/753834288511713303/82e43c1418a21926dd61d71f32a6222e.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

_28-Apr-22 01:08 PM_:

I just want to compliment what @mitch (üçî, üçî) said with the problems of the transcription - quantification periods are time sensitive, if 2 weeks of community call praise are dished at the same time, they will appear to belong to the same period and this is causing confusion to quantifiers. - @Mount Manu expressed a lack of motivation to do this task, which I think we can all agree to be tedious. He also said it's a non-rewarded task - you can speak more on it Manu, but it's important for us to look at how people are feeling about what they are doing - so it's an unpleasant task that represents a single point of failure for a large data set - + the point that Mitch brought up, the praise people dish when they are on a rush has been quite low quality and generalized


but we don't want to lose the beauty and excitement and high vibes the praise round has in the community call, so how could we slowly request that people type their praise, and be more mindful of it?

@griff (üíú, üíú)

@Tam2140

<h3>liviade <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/480023322080444427/5749f33d32f3d2bf7084c18540ead477.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

I just want to compliment what @mitch (üçî, üçî) said with the problems of the transcription - quantification periods are time sensitive, if 2 weeks of community call praise are dished at the same time, they will appear to belong to the same period and this is causing confusion to quantifiers. - @Mount Manu expressed a lack of motivation to do this task, which I think we can all agree to be tedious. He also said it's a non-rewarded task - you can speak more on it Manu, but it's important for us to look at how people are feeling about what they are doing - so it's an unpleasant task that represents a single point of failure for a large data set - + the point that Mitch brought up, the praise people dish when they are on a rush has been quite low quality and generalized

_28-Apr-22 02:17 PM_:

we do the out-loud praise in the Giveth Community call but *also* everyone writes it in the channel. I think we could have a transition period where we just encourage that, but still have Algene (for example) as a backup for new people or people who forget, and then just phase out the idea that someone will be writing it down for you.

I write my call praise anyway, but just... not in the channel. I think a lot of people do this.

<h3>liviade <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/480023322080444427/5749f33d32f3d2bf7084c18540ead477.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

I just want to compliment what @mitch (üçî, üçî) said with the problems of the transcription - quantification periods are time sensitive, if 2 weeks of community call praise are dished at the same time, they will appear to belong to the same period and this is causing confusion to quantifiers. - @Mount Manu expressed a lack of motivation to do this task, which I think we can all agree to be tedious. He also said it's a non-rewarded task - you can speak more on it Manu, but it's important for us to look at how people are feeling about what they are doing - so it's an unpleasant task that represents a single point of failure for a large data set - + the point that Mitch brought up, the praise people dish when they are on a rush has been quite low quality and generalized

_20-May-22 08:04 AM_:

Want to share the Amazon leadership principle that is directly related to our conversation about spending in the @Stewards Council yesterday. **Frugality** Accomplish more with less. Constraints breed resourcefulness, self-sufficiency, and invention. There are no extra points for growing headcount, budget size, or fixed expense. All are excellent principles to live by, in general, but that one is most timely to our discussions. [https://www.amazon.jobs/en/principles](https://www.amazon.jobs/en/principles)

Amazon's global career site

![https://static.amazon.jobs/global_images/2/images/Jobs_thumbnailV2.jpg?1554491962](https://static.amazon.jobs/global_images/2/images/Jobs_thumbnailV2.jpg?1554491962)

![https://cdn.discordapp.com/emojis/835016327542210560.png](https://cdn.discordapp.com/emojis/835016327542210560.png)

Hi folks, A few other researchers from the Metagovernance Project have recently been studying the TEC constitution as part of a larger research project on the constitutions of Web3 funded by the Filecoin Foundation. We‚Äôve stored and coded up the constitution within our model along with many others and are trying to understand how to support more and better constitutions within Web3. Could someone please fill out this short survey for Metagov on how you constructed yours? <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f64f.png" width=50 height=50> <img src="https://twemoji.maxcdn.com/2/72x72/1f33b.png" width=20 height=20>

Calling all @Stewards and all that wish to join in the introspection! Why do we do a Retrospective at the end of every Sprint?

**Because Scrum is founded on empiricism and lean thinking. Empiricism asserts that knowledge comes from experience and making decisions based on what is observed. Lean thinking reduces waste and focuses on the essentials.**

<h3>Tam2140 <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/751417874886688798/2654f95ffa0a47282c16ea274733b86d.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

The main objective of the Community Stewards WG is to provide visibility across all of the separate work streams such that all Stewards walk forward together in lockstep to reach our high level TEC goals. Our weekly meetings are a place to check-in on the temperature of the community, to resolve blockers, to raise questions that affect the Stewards or the members of our community and to solve them with the collective intelligence. We follow a Scrum framework and have a 2-week Sprint cadence. WG Lead: @Tam2140 Discussions happen on #stewards channel All calls happen on #stewards voice channel Weekly call: Tuesday at 7pm CET Council call: Every other Thursday at 6pm CET Sprint Retrospective: Every other Thursday at 6pm CET Sprint Planning: Every other Friday at 6pm CET Stewards Manifesto

[https://docs.google.com/document/d/1cqdURiW7Qv50J_Ha9FLr9IvdqnZGuhlsffL6O1ivHnA

_04-Jun-22 01:38 AM_:

Hey @Stewards ! I'm loving the Proposal Inverter, I've had ideas on this for a while. I'm very much in favour of anything that helps DAOs to move across to systems that support good ideas, and the Proposal Inverter is a Rolls Royce of a solution, which will generate lots of data. It is possible, though, to get a much simpler VW Beetle version in the short term, creating a Notion table, and showing a proposal moving through the following stages and statuses: Idea ‚û°Ô∏è Team ‚û°Ô∏è Proposal ‚û°Ô∏è Project ‚û°Ô∏è Product ‚û°Ô∏è Data The Notion would point to eg Google Drives where related documentation for that stage can be stored. Why do this and not just wait for the Rolls Royce to show up? Getting into the mindset early would be an advantage to all DAO members, because the effect of defining and publicising project roles and so forth is an important skill set, and can be developed with either variety of tool, although I acknowledge the PI will offer stepped stages, probably meaning greater accessibility to more folk, and substantial quantities of data, which of course then has intrinsic value for research. I'd be interested to discuss this more with a TEC steward. (edited)

<h3>innov8tor3 <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/530682470232883210/193353ccfcbc44b9892dbb7a5862c455.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

Hey @Stewards ! I'm loving the Proposal Inverter, I've had ideas on this for a while. I'm very much in favour of anything that helps DAOs to move across to systems that support good ideas, and the Proposal Inverter is a Rolls Royce of a solution, which will generate lots of data. It is possible, though, to get a much simpler VW Beetle version in the short term, creating a Notion table, and showing a proposal moving through the following stages and statuses: Idea ‚û°Ô∏è Team ‚û°Ô∏è Proposal ‚û°Ô∏è Project ‚û°Ô∏è Product ‚û°Ô∏è Data The Notion would point to eg Google Drives where related documentation for that stage can be stored. Why do this and not just wait for the Rolls Royce to show up? Getting into the mindset early would be an advantage to all DAO members, because the effect of defining and publicising project roles and so forth is an important skill set, and can be developed with either variety of tool, although I acknowledge the PI will offer stepped stages, probably meaning greater accessibility to more folk, and substantial quantities of data, which of course then has intrinsic value for research. I'd be interested to discuss this more with a TEC steward.  (edited)

_05-Jun-22 02:34 PM_:

Heyy, thank you for the comment! Actually we are using kind of VW Beetle in proposal inverter‚Äôs development. Thanks to @ygg_anderson ‚Äòs initiation we embraced the dogfooding building model (a product built by the idea of the product). We are using excel sheets to mimic proposal inverter mechanism through off chain interactions. This video may help understand our building Philosophy:

[https://youtu.be/x2gf-UUiEL0](https://youtu.be/x2gf-UUiEL0)

[The DAOist](https://www.youtube.com/channel/UCSm6Gic3HQHoFd7k3x8LNkQ)

The DAOist CDMX: The Proposal Inverter: A dogfooding model for DAO ...

The DAOist Mexico is mainly focused on bringing DAO culture to the local communities. An entire 2-day event designed for entry-level web3 contributors locals, with talks in Spanish, sharing art and knowledge from the DAOverse in one of the biggest capitals of the world.

![https://i.ytimg.com/vi/x2gf-UUiEL0/maxresdefault.jpg](https://i.ytimg.com/vi/x2gf-UUiEL0/maxresdefault.jpg)

(Starting from 10.00 )

TEC Sprint Retrospective Agenda

TEC Sprint Retrospective Scrum Theory : Scrum is founded on empiricism and lean thinking. Empiricism asserts that knowledge comes from experience and making decisions based on what is observed. Lean thinking reduces waste and focuses on the essentials. Purpose of the Retrospective : To plans...

[https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/kpxZc7dUkipJBOF_UuBq5D1jrflIxRch7yOcprO2VWvKuZYWvVH9guEeIFyqHc-0JeRievArZsIOnw=w1200-h630-p](https://lh6.googleusercontent.com/kpxZc7dUkipJBOF_UuBq5D1jrflIxRch7yOcprO2VWvKuZYWvVH9guEeIFyqHc-0JeRievArZsIOnw=w1200-h630-p)

_06-Jul-22 05:38 PM_:

I just got a message from someone I used to work with who happens to be a Hatcher. They were asking me why the TEC is asking for more money from them. Here's what they said (I got their permission to share this): So why do you want more money from us? or maybe I don't "get" what is going on but I felt like I did all this work to contribute like $1000+ to the hatch - and I could bearly do it with metamask etc - (and gosh I really hope I still have the keys etc - cause you know crypto and normal people and normal UX don't go really well together). - why would I be asked for more money " to stay a member" I thought I "bought" into a DAO - was new to me that some how I could get degraded out - when I "bought" the tokens.

![https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/810180622634844206/994356623667638302/unknown.png](https://cdn.discordapp.com/attachments/810180622634844206/994356623667638302/unknown.png)

I asked them to forward the message they had received and it was an email. See attached. We have to be careful about these kinds of messages. I know that we're (justifiably) excited about the ABC, but this message left at least one person very confused. It also negatively impacted their impression of the TEC. In this case, it happens to be someone who is fairly influential in the broader open source world beyond Web3. (edited)

This email came on the heels of a request for Trusted Seed membership payments too, so that is exacerbating the problem and adding to real confusion: ----- mmm... i guess I am confused So what did I "buy" membership in? or how do these relate - are they related?

I guess I was confused cause I didn't really track they were two different things - since I was walked through what I needed to do to join/buy tokens... then I'm like "why am I being shaken down for money"

This left a really bad taste for the TEC with this person. I just happen to have known them, so they reached out to me to find out what this was. When we send messages to token holders, it's really important to first run them by others as part of the advice process. That's what we did with the update to token holders a few weeks ago, and it made the message way stronger. I'm always willing to have a look at stuff like this before it goes out (and I'm sure there are others who'd be willing to as well). This is especially true when the message is going to token holders. We're working so hard to bolster the connection with them; the last thing we want to do is confuse or alienate them. (edited)

<h3>Gideonro <img src="https://cdn.discordapp.com/avatars/343470788491476992/4ee572be9bb18b06c9292a97a2016cee.png" width=25 height=25></h3>

This left a really bad taste for the TEC with this person. I just happen to have known them, so they reached out to me to find out what this was. When we send messages to token holders, it's really important to first run them by others as part of the advice process. That's what we did with the update to token holders a few weeks ago, and it made the message way stronger. I'm always willing to have a look at stuff like this before it goes out (and I'm sure there are others who'd be willing to as well). This is especially true when the message is going to token holders. We're working so hard to bolster the connection with them; the last thing we want to do is confuse or alienate them.  (edited)
